		<script>    
    let slideIndex = 0;
    let slideTimer;

    function startTimer() {
        // เช็คว่ามี Slider ในหน้าหรือไม่
        if (document.getElementsByClassName("hero-slide").length > 0) {
            slideTimer = setInterval(function(){ moveSlide(1); }, 5000); 
        }
    }

    function moveSlide(n) {
        let slides = document.getElementsByClassName("hero-slide");
        if (slides.length === 0) return;

        slideIndex += n;

        if (slideIndex >= slides.length) { slideIndex = 0; }
        if (slideIndex < 0) { slideIndex = slides.length - 1; }

        for (let i = 0; i < slides.length; i++) {
            slides[i].className = slides[i].className.replace(" active", "");
        }
        slides[slideIndex].className += " active";

        clearInterval(slideTimer);
        startTimer();
    }

    window.onload = startTimer;

<script src="https://www.thainews.live/wp-content/themes/generatepress/assets/js/back-to-top.min.js?ver=3.6.1" id="generate-back-to-top-js"></script>
<script>    (function() {
        const allowedDomains = ["wikipedia.org","google.com","facebook.com","youtube.com","twitter.com","shopee.co.th","lazada.co.th"];

        function getCleanHostname(url) {
            try {
                return new URL(url).hostname.replace(/^www\./, '');
            } catch (e) {
                return '';
            }
        }

        const currentHost = getCleanHostname(window.location.href);

        function processLinks() {
            var links = document.querySelectorAll('a');
            
            links.forEach(function(link) {
                if (!link.href || link.href.indexOf('java' + 'script') === 0 || link.href.indexOf('#') === 0) return;

                var linkHost = getCleanHostname(link.href);

                // Internal Link Check
                if (linkHost === currentHost || linkHost.endsWith('.' + currentHost)) {
                    if (link.hasAttribute('target')) {
                        link.removeAttribute('target'); 
                    }
                    link.setAttribute('target', '_self');
                    link.removeAttribute('rel');
                } else {
                    // External Link
                    link.setAttribute('target', '_blank');
                    var isTrusted = false;
                    for (var i = 0; i < allowedDomains.length; i++) {
                        if (linkHost.indexOf(allowedDomains[i]) !== -1) {
                            isTrusted = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                    if (isTrusted) {
                        link.setAttribute('rel', 'noopener');
                    } else {
                        link.setAttribute('rel', 'nofollow noreferrer noopener');
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        // Run Logic
        if(document.readyState === 'loading') {
            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', processLinks);
        } else {
            processLinks();
        }
        window.addEventListener('load', processLinks);

        // Click Intercept (ไม้ตาย)
        document.body.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            var link = e.target.closest('a');
            if (!link || !link.href) return;
            var linkHost = getCleanHostname(link.href);
            if (linkHost === currentHost || linkHost.endsWith('.' + currentHost)) {
                 if (link.target === '_blank') {
                     e.preventDefault();
                     window.location.href = link.href;
                 }
            }
        }, true);
    })();</script><script>
